    <script>
     var customCarousel = {
        createSlides: function (slide, indexNum) {
            var li = document.createElement("li");
            var a = document.createElement("a");
            var imgDiv = document.createElement("div");
            var img = document.createElement("img");
            var textDiv = document.createElement("div");
            var textDivInner = document.createElement("div");
            var h3 = document.createElement("h3");
            var p = document.createElement("p");
            var time = document.createElement("p");
            li.classList.add("custom__slide", "all__access__card");
            a.classList.add("all__access__card__link");
            imgDiv.classList.add("carousel__card__img__container");
            img.classList.add("carousel__card__img");
            textDiv.classList.add("carousel__card__text");
            textDivInner.classList.add("carousel__card__text__inner");
            h3.classList.add("carousel__card__header");
            p.classList.add("carousel__card__para");
            time.classList.add("carousel__card__timeframe");
            a.setAttribute("href", slide.link);
            img.setAttribute("src", slide.imgSrc);
            img.setAttribute("alt", slide.header);
            h3.textContent = slide.header;
            p.textContent = slide.para;
            time.textContent = slide.timeframe;
            imgDiv.appendChild(img);
            a.appendChild(imgDiv);
            textDivInner.appendChild(h3);
            textDivInner.appendChild(p);
            textDivInner.appendChild(time);
            textDiv.appendChild(textDivInner);
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-zone4", slide.zone4);
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-label", slide.zone4);
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-position", "carousel-all-access-" + (indexNum + 1));
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-impression", "promotion");
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-category", "allaccess");
            a.setAttribute("data-bb-action", "promotionClick");
            a.appendChild(textDiv);
            li.appendChild(a);
            return li;
        },
        randomize: function (slides) {
            return null;
        },
        setCarousel: function (dat) {
            var carouselOuter = document.querySelector(dat.className);
            carouselOuter.setAttribute("data-bb-zone3", dat.zone3);
        },
        initialize: function (data, slides) {
            customCarousel.setCarousel(data);
            var carouselOuter = document.querySelector(data.className).querySelector(".carousel__slides");
            var i;
            for (i = 0; i < slides.length; i++) {
                var slide = customCarousel.createSlides(slides[i], i);
                carouselOuter.appendChild(slide);
            }
            customCarousel.randomize(carouselOuter);
            var slider = tns({
                container: carouselOuter,
                items: 1,
                slideBy: 'page',
                arrowKeys: true,
                mode: "carousel",
                gutter: 10,
                carousel__dots: carouselOuter,
                navPosition: "bottom",
                controlsText: ["", ""],
                responsive: data.responsive,
                autoplay: false
            });
            var prevbutton = carouselOuter.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelectorAll("[data-controls='prev'")[0];
            var nextButton = carouselOuter.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelectorAll("[data-controls='next'")[0];
            var info = slider.getInfo(),
            currentSlide = info.displayIndex;
            if (currentSlide === 1) {
                prevbutton.classList.add("carousel__hide__control");
            } else if (currentSlide !== 1) {
                prevbutton.classList.remove("carousel__hide__control");
            }
            nextButton.onclick = function () {
                var info = slider.getInfo(),
                currentSlide = info.displayIndex;
                prevbutton.classList.remove("carousel__hide__control");
            };
        }
    };
    </script>
